[30;1m29 | [0m[35m    several workarounds for locking files. For more details, refer to the `Medium blog post`_.[0m

[30;1m29 | [0m[35mclass _TreeNode:[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m    # This is a class to represent the tree of search space.[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m    # A tree node has three states:[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m    # 1. Unexpanded. This is represented by children=None.[0m

[30;1m35 | [0m[35m    # 3. Normal node. It has a param_name and non-empty children.[0m
